<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">We at PowerQ Test & Tag Melbourne believe in making relations
</h2> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-f4144c7 elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="f4144c7" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p>Based in Melbourne, PowerQ Test & Tag Melbourne offers <strong><a href="https://www.powerq.com.au/electrical-test-and-tag-in-melbourne/">electrical testing and tagging</a></strong> services in Melbourne with full compliance to test and tag regulations that apply for Victoria. We are an experienced team of smart and skilled professionals, with full public liability cover and competence in test and tag services. We assure you complete peace of mind when you engage us as we follow all test and tag regulations that apply to your industry.We pride ourselves on delivering prompt, reliable, and affordable services tailored to meet your specific needs. Trust PowerQ Test & Tag Melbourne to ensure the safety and compliance of your electrical equipment.</p> </div>

<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default"> Smoke alarms are compulsory in every home</h2> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-7a84b07 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="7a84b07" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">By law, all residential properties must have working smoke alarms complying with Australian Standards AS 3786.</h2> </div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-2a822f8 e-flex e-con-boxed wpr-particle-no wpr-jarallax-no wpr-parallax-no wpr-sticky-section-no wpr-column-slider-no wpr-equal-height-no e-con e-parent" data-id="2a822f8" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container">
<div class="e-con-inner">
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-f561c76 e-con-full e-transform e-flex wpr-particle-no wpr-jarallax-no wpr-parallax-no wpr-sticky-section-no wpr-column-slider-no wpr-equal-height-no e-con e-child" data-id="f561c76" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container" data-settings="{&quot;background_background&quot;:&quot;classic&quot;,&quot;_transform_translateY_effect_hover&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;size&quot;:-3,&quot;sizes&quot;:[]},&quot;_transform_translateX_effect_hover&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;size&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;sizes&quot;:[]},&quot;_transform_translateX_effect_hover_tablet&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;size&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;sizes&quot;:[]},&quot;_transform_translateX_effect_hover_mobile&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;size&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;sizes&quot;:[]},&quot;_transform_translateY_effect_hover_tablet&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;size&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;sizes&quot;:[]},&quot;_transform_translateY_effect_hover_mobile&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;size&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;sizes&quot;:[]}}">

<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p>Residential homes constructed after 1 August 1997, or homes which have undergone a major renovation or extension, must have smoke alarms connected to 240-volt mains power with battery backup.</p> </div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-3aac02d e-con-full e-transform e-flex wpr-particle-no wpr-jarallax-no wpr-parallax-no wpr-sticky-section-no wpr-column-slider-no wpr-equal-height-no e-con e-child" data-id="3aac02d" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container" data-settings="{&quot;background_background&quot;:&quot;classic&quot;,&quot;_transform_translateY_effect_hover&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;size&quot;:-3,&quot;sizes&quot;:[]},&quot;_transform_translateX_effect_hover&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;size&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;sizes&quot;:[]},&quot;_transform_translateX_effect_hover_tablet&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;size&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;sizes&quot;:[]},&quot;_transform_translateX_effect_hover_mobile&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;size&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;sizes&quot;:[]},&quot;_transform_translateY_effect_hover_tablet&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;size&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;sizes&quot;:[]},&quot;_transform_translateY_effect_hover_mobile&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;size&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;sizes&quot;:[]}}">

<div class="elementor-icon-wrapper">
<div class="elementor-icon">

<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p>Residential homes constructed before 1 August 1997 may have battery-operated smoke alarms.</p> </div>
</div>

<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-807160f e-con-full e-transform e-flex wpr-particle-no wpr-jarallax-no wpr-parallax-no wpr-sticky-section-no wpr-column-slider-no wpr-equal-height-no e-con e-child" data-id="807160f" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container" data-settings="{&quot;background_background&quot;:&quot;classic&quot;,&quot;_transform_translateY_effect_hover&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;size&quot;:-3,&quot;sizes&quot;:[]},&quot;_transform_translateX_effect_hover&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;size&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;sizes&quot;:[]},&quot;_transform_translateX_effect_hover_tablet&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;size&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;sizes&quot;:[]},&quot;_transform_translateX_effect_hover_mobile&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;size&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;sizes&quot;:[]},&quot;_transform_translateY_effect_hover_tablet&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;size&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;sizes&quot;:[]},&quot;_transform_translateY_effect_hover_mobile&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;size&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;sizes&quot;:[]}}">

<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<div class="elementor-icon-wrapper">

<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p>Residential homes constructed after 1 May 2014, or homes which have undergone a major renovation or extension, must have smoke alarms interconnected (if there is a requirement for more than one smoke alarm).</p> </div>

<div class="e-con-inner">
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-edda829 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="edda829" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">New Smoke Alarm Laws in Victoria. The recently changed Residential Tenancy Regulations has made it mandatory for landlords to conduct regular gas and electric safety checks on their rental properties. Gas and electric safety checks must be done at least every 2 years and smoke alarms must be tested annually.
</h2> </div>
</div>

<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-a547fe0 e-flex e-con-boxed wpr-particle-no wpr-jarallax-no wpr-parallax-no wpr-sticky-section-no wpr-column-slider-no wpr-equal-height-no e-con e-parent" data-id="a547fe0" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container" data-settings="{&quot;background_background&quot;:&quot;classic&quot;}">

<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-100764f elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="100764f" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Smoke alarm facts</h2> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-4ff713c elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="4ff713c" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">If you don’t have a working smoke alarm installed in your home and a fire occurs:</h2> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-52046f9 elementor-view-framed elementor-position-inline-start elementor-mobile-position-inline-start elementor-shape-circle elementor-widget elementor-widget-icon-box" data-id="52046f9" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="icon-box.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<div class="elementor-icon-box-wrapper">

<div class="elementor-icon-box-icon">
<span class="elementor-icon">
<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 640 512"><path d="M288 350.1l0 1.9-32 0c-17.7 0-32 14.3-32 32l0 64 0 24c0 22.1-17.9 40-40 40l-24 0-31.9 0c-1.5 0-3-.1-4.5-.2c-1.2 .1-2.4 .2-3.6 .2l-16 0c-22.1 0-40-17.9-40-40l0-112c0-.9 0-1.9 .1-2.8l0-69.7-32 0c-18 0-32-14-32-32.1c0-9 3-17 10-24L266.4 8c7-7 15-8 22-8s15 2 21 7L447.3 128.1c-12.3-1-25 3-34.8 11.7c-35.4 31.6-65.6 67.7-87.3 102.8C304.3 276.5 288 314.9 288 350.1zM480 512c-88.4 0-160-71.6-160-160c0-76.7 62.5-144.7 107.2-179.4c5-3.9 10.9-5.8 16.8-5.8c7.9-.1 16 3.1 22 9.2l46 46 11.3-11.3c11.7-11.7 30.6-12.7 42.3-1C624.5 268 640 320.2 640 352c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160zm64-111.8c0-36.5-37-73-54.8-88.4c-5.4-4.7-13.1-4.7-18.5 0C453 327.1 416 363.6 416 400.2c0 35.3 28.7 64 64 64s64-28.7 64-64z"></path></svg> </span>

<h3 class="elementor-icon-box-title">
<span >
You are more likely to incur property loss and damage. </span>
</h3>
<p class="elementor-icon-box-description">

<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-64ace6b elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="64ace6b" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">All smoke alarms:</h2> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-d07c22f elementor-view-framed elementor-position-inline-start elementor-mobile-position-inline-start elementor-shape-circle elementor-widget elementor-widget-icon-box" data-id="d07c22f" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="icon-box.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<div class="elementor-icon-box-wrapper">

<div class="e-con-inner">
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-d37d516 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="d37d516" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Smoke alarms should not be located in kitchens and bathrooms.</h2> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-4aff9c8 elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="4aff9c8" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p><strong>1.</strong>  The Australasian Fire and Emergency Services Council (AFAC) recommends smoke alarms be replaced with interconnected alarms in all sleeping areas, living spaces, paths of travel (hallways, stairways) and garages if they are under the home’s main roof.</p> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-50696b4 elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="50696b4" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p><strong>2.</strong> New Smoke Alarm Laws in Victoria. The recently changed Residential Tenancy Regulations has made it mandatory for landlords to conduct regular gas and electric safety checks on their rental properties. Gas and electric safety checks must be done at least every 2 years and smoke alarms must be tested annually.</p> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-c50334b elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="c50334b" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Smoke alarms powered by 240-volt mains must be interconnected by an electrician.</h2> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-3d70e0e elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="3d70e0e" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p>3. Battery operated, including long life battery alarms, can be interconnected by purchasing interconnected wireless smoke alarms. Electricians are not required to install these smoke alarms.</p> </div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-5af7cf4 e-flex e-con-boxed wpr-particle-no wpr-jarallax-no wpr-parallax-no wpr-sticky-section-no wpr-column-slider-no wpr-equal-height-no e-con e-parent" data-id="5af7cf4" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container" data-settings="{&quot;background_background&quot;:&quot;classic&quot;}">
<div class="e-con-inner">
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-7b68d04 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="7b68d04" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Smoke alarms must be installed in:</h2> </div>
</div>

<h3 class="elementor-icon-box-title">
<span >
Buildings used for short term accommodation </span>
</h3>
<p class="elementor-icon-box-description">
(boarding house, guest house, hostel, bed and breakfast accommodation, cabins in caravan parks, tourist parks, holiday resorts, and similar tourist accommodation Victorian fire and rescue services recommend smoke alarms connected to 240-volt mains power with a battery backup or alarms powered by a 10 year long-life battery. When more than one smoke alarm is installed, they should be interconnected so that when any alarm activates, all smoke alarms will sound. </p>

<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Frequently asked questions:</h2> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-4117a8b elementor-widget elementor-widget-n-accordion" data-id="4117a8b" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-settings="{&quot;default_state&quot;:&quot;expanded&quot;,&quot;max_items_expended&quot;:&quot;one&quot;,&quot;n_accordion_animation_duration&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;ms&quot;,&quot;size&quot;:400,&quot;sizes&quot;:[]}}" data-widget_type="nested-accordion.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<div class="e-n-accordion" aria-label="Accordion. Open links with Enter or Space, close with Escape, and navigate with Arrow Keys">
<details id="e-n-accordion-item-6820" class="e-n-accordion-item" open>
<summary class="e-n-accordion-item-title" data-accordion-index="1" tabindex="0" aria-expanded="true" aria-controls="e-n-accordion-item-6820" >
<span class='e-n-accordion-item-title-header'><div class="e-n-accordion-item-title-text"> Why should I test my smoke alarm? </div></span>
<span class='e-n-accordion-item-title-icon'>
<span class='e-opened' ><svg aria-hidden="true" class="e-font-icon-svg e-fas-angle-up" viewBox="0 0 320 512" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M177 159.7l136 136c9.4 9.4 9.4 24.6 0 33.9l-22.6 22.6c-9.4 9.4-24.6 9.4-33.9 0L160 255.9l-96.4 96.4c-9.4 9.4-24.6 9.4-33.9 0L7 329.7c-9.4-9.4-9.4-24.6 0-33.9l136-136c9.4-9.5 24.6-9.5 34-.1z"></path></svg></span>
<span class='e-closed'><svg aria-hidden="true" class="e-font-icon-svg e-fas-chevron-down" viewBox="0 0 448 512" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M207.029 381.476L12.686 187.132c-9.373-9.373-9.373-24.569 0-33.941l22.667-22.667c9.357-9.357 24.522-9.375 33.901-.04L224 284.505l154.745-154.021c9.379-9.335 24.544-9.317 33.901.04l22.667 22.667c9.373 9.373 9.373 24.569 0 33.941L240.971 381.476c-9.373 9.372-24.569 9.372-33.942 0z"></path></svg></span>
</span>

</summary>
<div role="region" aria-labelledby="e-n-accordion-item-6820" class="elementor-element elementor-element-ae10b51 e-con-full e-flex wpr-particle-no wpr-jarallax-no wpr-parallax-no wpr-sticky-section-no wpr-column-slider-no wpr-equal-height-no e-con e-child" data-id="ae10b51" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container">
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-f386b2c elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="f386b2c" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p>A working smoke alarm is your first line of defence in the event of a fire. You should test your smoke alarm regularly to ensure the battery is not flat and that the alarm will sound when you need it most.</p> </div>
</div>
</div>
</details>
<details id="e-n-accordion-item-6821" class="e-n-accordion-item" >
<summary class="e-n-accordion-item-title" data-accordion-index="2" tabindex="-1" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="e-n-accordion-item-6821" >
<span class='e-n-accordion-item-title-header'><div class="e-n-accordion-item-title-text"> Why does my smoke alarm beep once every 60 seconds or intermittently? </div></span>
<span class='e-n-accordion-item-title-icon'>
<span class='e-opened' ><svg aria-hidden="true" class="e-font-icon-svg e-fas-angle-up" viewBox="0 0 320 512" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M177 159.7l136 136c9.4 9.4 9.4 24.6 0 33.9l-22.6 22.6c-9.4 9.4-24.6 9.4-33.9 0L160 255.9l-96.4 96.4c-9.4 9.4-24.6 9.4-33.9 0L7 329.7c-9.4-9.4-9.4-24.6 0-33.9l136-136c9.4-9.5 24.6-9.5 34-.1z"></path></svg></span>
<span class='e-closed'><svg aria-hidden="true" class="e-font-icon-svg e-fas-chevron-down" viewBox="0 0 448 512" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M207.029 381.476L12.686 187.132c-9.373-9.373-9.373-24.569 0-33.941l22.667-22.667c9.357-9.357 24.522-9.375 33.901-.04L224 284.505l154.745-154.021c9.379-9.335 24.544-9.317 33.901.04l22.667 22.667c9.373 9.373 9.373 24.569 0 33.941L240.971 381.476c-9.373 9.372-24.569 9.372-33.942 0z"></path></svg></span>
</span>

</summary>
<div role="region" aria-labelledby="e-n-accordion-item-6821" class="elementor-element elementor-element-555cd17 e-con-full e-flex wpr-particle-no wpr-jarallax-no wpr-parallax-no wpr-sticky-section-no wpr-column-slider-no wpr-equal-height-no e-con e-child" data-id="555cd17" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container">
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-fd78445 elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="fd78445" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p>This could mean that the battery is going flat and needs replacing.<br /><strong>Note: Replace the entire smoke alarm if it still beeps after installing a new battery.</strong></p> </div>
</div>
</div>
</details>
<details id="e-n-accordion-item-6822" class="e-n-accordion-item" >
<summary class="e-n-accordion-item-title" data-accordion-index="3" tabindex="-1" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="e-n-accordion-item-6822" >
<span class='e-n-accordion-item-title-header'><div class="e-n-accordion-item-title-text"> Why do 240-volt smoke alarms have a battery? </div></span>
<span class='e-n-accordion-item-title-icon'>
<span class='e-opened' ><svg aria-hidden="true" class="e-font-icon-svg e-fas-angle-up" viewBox="0 0 320 512" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M177 159.7l136 136c9.4 9.4 9.4 24.6 0 33.9l-22.6 22.6c-9.4 9.4-24.6 9.4-33.9 0L160 255.9l-96.4 96.4c-9.4 9.4-24.6 9.4-33.9 0L7 329.7c-9.4-9.4-9.4-24.6 0-33.9l136-136c9.4-9.5 24.6-9.5 34-.1z"></path></svg></span>
<span class='e-closed'><svg aria-hidden="true" class="e-font-icon-svg e-fas-chevron-down" viewBox="0 0 448 512" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M207.029 381.476L12.686 187.132c-9.373-9.373-9.373-24.569 0-33.941l22.667-22.667c9.357-9.357 24.522-9.375 33.901-.04L224 284.505l154.745-154.021c9.379-9.335 24.544-9.317 33.901.04l22.667 22.667c9.373 9.373 9.373 24.569 0 33.941L240.971 381.476c-9.373 9.372-24.569 9.372-33.942 0z"></path></svg></span>
</span>

</summary>
<div role="region" aria-labelledby="e-n-accordion-item-6822" class="elementor-element elementor-element-53e0b35 e-con-full e-flex wpr-particle-no wpr-jarallax-no wpr-parallax-no wpr-sticky-section-no wpr-column-slider-no wpr-equal-height-no e-con e-child" data-id="53e0b35" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container">
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-38021df elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="38021df" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p>240-volt smoke alarms connected to mains power are required to have a battery to provide back-up power in the event of a power outage.</p> </div>
</div>
</div>
</details>
<details id="e-n-accordion-item-6823" class="e-n-accordion-item" >
<summary class="e-n-accordion-item-title" data-accordion-index="4" tabindex="-1" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="e-n-accordion-item-6823" >
<span class='e-n-accordion-item-title-header'><div class="e-n-accordion-item-title-text"> What can I do if my smoke alarm operates every time I make toast or have a shower? </div></span>
<span class='e-n-accordion-item-title-icon'>
<span class='e-opened' ><svg aria-hidden="true" class="e-font-icon-svg e-fas-angle-up" viewBox="0 0 320 512" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M177 159.7l136 136c9.4 9.4 9.4 24.6 0 33.9l-22.6 22.6c-9.4 9.4-24.6 9.4-33.9 0L160 255.9l-96.4 96.4c-9.4 9.4-24.6 9.4-33.9 0L7 329.7c-9.4-9.4-9.4-24.6 0-33.9l136-136c9.4-9.5 24.6-9.5 34-.1z"></path></svg></span>
<span class='e-closed'><svg aria-hidden="true" class="e-font-icon-svg e-fas-chevron-down" viewBox="0 0 448 512" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M207.029 381.476L12.686 187.132c-9.373-9.373-9.373-24.569 0-33.941l22.667-22.667c9.357-9.357 24.522-9.375 33.901-.04L224 284.505l154.745-154.021c9.379-9.335 24.544-9.317 33.901.04l22.667 22.667c9.373 9.373 9.373 24.569 0 33.941L240.971 381.476c-9.373 9.372-24.569 9.372-33.942 0z"></path></svg></span>
</span>

</summary>
<div role="region" aria-labelledby="e-n-accordion-item-6823" class="elementor-element elementor-element-605fc5c e-con-full e-flex wpr-particle-no wpr-jarallax-no wpr-parallax-no wpr-sticky-section-no wpr-column-slider-no wpr-equal-height-no e-con e-child" data-id="605fc5c" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container">
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-213cc6b elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="213cc6b" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p>Do not remove the battery. A primary reason why smoke alarms do not operate when needed is because batteries have been removed after repeated false alarms. What you should do is:</p><ul><li>Check the type of smoke alarm installed – if it is an ionisation type, consider replacing it with a photoelectric type smoke alarm.</li><li>Consider installing an exhaust fan in the kitchen or bathroom.</li><li>Consider relocating the smoke alarm away from the kitchen or bathroom.</li></ul> </div>
</div>
</div>
</details>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-e136f04 e-flex e-con-boxed wpr-particle-no wpr-jarallax-no wpr-parallax-no wpr-sticky-section-no wpr-column-slider-no wpr-equal-height-no e-con e-parent" data-id="e136f04" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container" data-settings="{&quot;background_background&quot;:&quot;classic&quot;}">
<div class="e-con-inner">
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-d3921ce elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="d3921ce" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Rental Properties:</h2> </div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-495fff3 elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="495fff3" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
<p>Residential rental providers are responsible for fitting smoke alarms in rented properties.1</p><p>Victoria’s Residential Tenancies Act, Section 68 (1), states “A residential rental provider must ensure that rented premises are provided and maintained in good repair.” A landlord must repair or replace a non-functioning smoke alarm once notified by the tenant.2</p><p>It is the responsibility of renters to test the smoke alarm each month and it is the responsibility of the landlord or owner to clean the smoke alarm and replace the battery annually (if applicable)</p><p>1. Consumer Affairs Victoria, Renting a home:<br />     A guide for tenants, p. 20, 32</p><p>2. Residential Tenancies Amendment Act 2018</p><p>3. Australasian Fire and Emergency Service</p><p>    Authorities Counsil,Smoke Alarm in Residential Accommodation, 2018, p. 4.</p> </div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-22ba375 e-flex e-con-boxed wpr-particle-no wpr-jarallax-no wpr-parallax-no wpr-sticky-section-no wpr-column-slider-no wpr-equal-height-no e-con e-parent" data-id="22ba375" data-element_type="container" data-e-type="container">
<div class="e-con-inner">

<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-87ef8b6 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="87ef8b6" data-element_type="widget" data-e-type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default">
<div class="elementor-widget-container">
